[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): This happens because you used a `BuildContext` that does not include the provider
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): of your choice. There are a few common scenarios:
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): - You added a new provider in your `main.dart` and performed a hot-reload.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   To fix, perform a hot-restart.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): - The provider you are trying to read is in a different route.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   Providers are "scoped". So if you insert of provider inside a route, then
[   +1 ms] I/flutter ( 9071):   other routes will not be able to access that provider.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[   +2 ms] I/flutter ( 9071): - You used a `BuildContext` that is an ancestor of the provider you are trying to read.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   Make sure that AdminImportAllPage is under your MultiProvider/Provider<AdminImportAllCubit>.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   This usually happens when you are creating a provider and trying to read it immediately.
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   For example, instead of:
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   ```
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):     return Provider<Example>(
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       create: (_) => Example(),
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       // Will throw a ProviderNotFoundError, because `context` is associated
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       // to the widget that is the parent of `Provider<Example>`
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       child: Text(context.watch<Example>().toString()),
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):     );
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   }
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   ```
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   consider using `builder` like so:
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071): 
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   ```
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):     return Provider<Example>(
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       create: (_) => Example(),
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       // we use `builder` to obtain a new `BuildContext` that has access to the provider
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):       builder: (context, child) {
[        ] I/flutter ( 9071):         // No longer throws
